<user_name>Ken Chew</user_name><time>1570856017042</time><Rating>5< /Rating><text>I was not expecting too much when I saw that not too many people rated the place on here, Yelp and 4 squares. <name>Mandi W<//name><Time>1577206490055< /Time><Rate>4< /Rate>< review>
If you need a new date spot, look no further!

Korean short ribs are to die for. They're perfectly cooked, only wish they came with more than four radishes and rice. You can buy rice and kimchi but no free banchan.

Their roast duck (half or full) was good too. Leg was horribly overcooked but the breast was amazingly medium rare and cooked to perfection.

Beef tartar and the trout crudo were both good appetizers, but if I had to choose one, it'd be the beef.

And the perilla leaves with shrimp were a nice starter for the evening.

Service is amazing, always clearing plates and filling glasses but never being overly attentive/ borderline annoying.

Overall, great new spot. Hope next time they're not out of the uni roe. ü§û</review>

0x808581a4b3b1d6cf:0xfd938090e8f27558<//gmapID>
<Response>None</Response><Pics>None< /Pics><Text>Fantastic delicate Korean fusion.<//Text><user_name>Peter Casey<//user_name>< userid>
106915665365545571095<//userid>
</record></dataset><record>
<pics>None< /pics>< text>
It was a high-end tasting course level of food at a friendly ambience and affordable price in SF. The attention to detail, freshness of each ingredient, and pleasant dining experience displayed a glimpse of the mastermind behind the new Korean restaurant, Ssal.

The appetizer started with some Lotus Chips and Halibut Crudo. The Halibut Crudo was pleasantly surprising with a light citrus taste from kumquat and swiss chard. Perfectly balanced sweetness and citrus taste.

Duck Liver Mousse also had a nice citrus taste with a Yuza glaze. Spring Onion Korean Pancake was very crispy and good, far from other soggy and mushy Korean pancakes that I've had before. Definitely add the pickled onion on top of the pancakes. It will pleasantly lighten up the taste.

Pork collar and beef short ribs were sooooooo good. It  melted in mouth with a nice amount of fat to coat the mouth with rich flavors. Also, they came with a choice of freshly picked greens from local farmers.

In summary, Ssal will bring Korean dining experience to another level in San Francisco. The modern twist of Korean food still paid homage to traditional Korean dining culture.< /text>

< Name>
Brenda Torres< /Name>
<Resp>None< /Resp><Review>Thank you San Joaquin Valley National Cemetery for making my father's service personal and putting me and my family at ease. Your staff was easy to work with and the service was lovely.

To anyone that has not done this please note the following for your mortuary: 1. Hearse should arrive 30 minutes prior to scheduled service. 2. Designated family member managing the service should also arrive 30 min prior to service. 3. Managing member will meet with the cemetery staff and finalize preparations. 4. Attendees will line up behind the hearse / transport vehicle and be taken to a designated area for your service. 5. The location we had was site B and it was an outdoor covered patio that would seat about 20 people with additional standing room. 6. Honor guard delivers your loved one along with additional family members as pall bears if desired. 7. Flag is folded and delivered to identified family member 8. Taps is played  9. Family or friends are allowed to speak for a few minutes (5-10) 10. You may then follow the transport vehicle to burial site. 11. Family and friends will wait behind a chained off area to observe their family member getting lowered and may return at 4pm that day. Please note you cannot stay for the entire covering.< /Review><GmapID>0x80919aa00fc9a3ad:0x3bf55bb30d7829b9< /GmapID>< pics>
None< /pics>

<response>None<//response>< review>
Finally had the opportunity to visit Tang & Noodle. I've been wanting to come here ever since it opened. The restaurant is located in a busy shopping plaza with other restaurants.

You can't miss it, it's in the front of the plaza.

Once we walked in, there is a sign indicating that you must sign in with the ipad (this just applies when they are busy). When we went, one of the staff members just greeted us and took  us to our table. Once we were seated, we were asked if we wanted hot or iced tea.  If it's your first time there, they take time to explain the menu.

We ordered the bone broth soup with purple rice and spicy soup with ramen. The broth was very tasty. We liked the bone broth more than the spicy one. The ramen is a high quality ramen that comes already cooked. The soups were so good that we paid very little attention to the banchan.

Everything was so good and I can't wait to go back again. We'll be ordering the meat dishes and musubi next time we go.</review>

< review>
We walked into the restaurant and was greeted immediately by a waitress across the room. There is a booth that allows you to check in or wait list through the Yelp app.  Very friendly customer service. We were seated and given plenty of time to order.  Food was great. The regular (not combo) meals were large and very filling. The side dishes are tasty as well. The fishcake has a bit more mushy texture compared to others, but tasted the same nonetheless.  In all, we enjoyed eating here and will come back!< /review>

1546546291264</Time>
< Rate>
4<//Rate>
<Text>Finally got to try this place after passing it a few times while back in Rowland Heights. I was always interested because of the combination deal they have, one Tang and one Noodle (or entree).

Love the concept of building your own soup bowl! I tried the spicy beef bone broth, as well as the regular that my brother ordered. The spicy one was just spicy enough to notice, but not so much that you couldn't stand to eat the soup. I opted for the meat and dumpling protein choice, which I actually wouldn't recommend because compared to the amount of meat you get with one of the other meat options, the dumplings don't really make up the volume, in my opinion. Though, if you like dumplings a lot go for it, because they're also pretty good! The unseasoned beef broth was pretty good, but I think if I were to go for a non-spicy option I'd go for the seasoned one.

I chose to get an entree to accompany my combo, and chose LA Galbi. It was definitely quality meat, and a really delicious sizzling plate. Next time, I hope to try one of the noodle dishes in order to try something a little different.

Since I split the combo with someone, I also got one of the musubis that they have--and they have a lot!!-- and was not disappointed! The anchovy musubi is delicious and I've never seen anything like it; I also really like that the filling is inside the rice, wrapped up neatly, instead of on top. Super good, and I could have definitely been happy making a meal of different ones! I'll definitely be back--there's so much to try, plus the staff is super friendly and helpful, and the restaurant itself is very clean and modern, definitely a standout spot even in a plaza full of eateries!< /Text>< Pics>
None</Pics>

<date>1531846112300< /date><Rate>5<//Rate><text>First time vising this recently opened restaurant.  When I saw the menu, I thought it was a little complicated but with the help from one of the staff members, got the system down in no minutes.  Basically, you first pick the soup base of your choice (beef bone soup / beef soup / spicy beef soup), then you pick the protein of your choice by going down the list, then you pick the carbs of your choice (rice (white v. purple) / noodle (ramen noodle v. rice noodle), then finally you decide whether you want to go combo with other entree items depending on how hungry you are.  I tried Yukgaejang (spicy beef soup) + Sokuh (mixed protein) + ramen noodle and combined that with Gochujang Spicy Squid Bulgogi.  How was it?  It was awesome!  The level of spiciness was just about right and the broth was not too greasy or heavy at all.  The best part was the ramen noodle!  It was cooked on a little harder side, just the way I always enjoy ramen.  I also tried Myulchi (Anchovy) musubi which was also good.  All staff members were super friendly.  For those Korean soup lovers, it's definitely a must go place!  Will definitely visit the place again soon, especially when I'm hung over^^< /text><pictures>None<//pictures><resp>None<//resp><gmap_id>0x80c32b63cf869f59:0x8c55d065a715075b<//gmap_id></record></dataset><record>
